### Subsection: 10.1c Resources and Support for Students

#### Academic Support

The MIT community recognizes the importance of academic support for students. The Institute provides a variety of resources to help students succeed in their academic pursuits. These resources include:

- The Academic Support and Advising Center (ASAC): The ASAC provides academic support services to all MIT undergraduate students. These services include individual and group tutoring, study skills workshops, and academic coaching.

- The Writing and Communication Center (WCC): The WCC provides writing and communication support to all MIT students. This includes help with writing assignments, presentations, and communication skills.

- The Office of Educational Innovation and Technology (OEIT): The OEIT supports the use of technology in education at MIT. This includes online learning platforms, educational software, and technology training for students.

#### Personal Support

In addition to academic support, MIT also provides personal support for students. This includes:

- The MIT Medical Department: The MIT Medical Department provides comprehensive health care services to all MIT students. This includes primary care, mental health services, and health education.

- The MIT Counseling and Mental Health Department: The MIT Counseling and Mental Health Department provides confidential counseling and mental health services to all MIT students. This includes individual and group counseling, crisis intervention, and mental health education.

- The MIT Chaplaincy: The MIT Chaplaincy provides spiritual and ethical support to all MIT students. This includes religious services, spiritual counseling, and interfaith dialogue.

#### Disability Support

MIT is committed to providing equal educational opportunities for all students. The Office of Disability Services (ODS) works with students who have disabilities to ensure equal access to MIT's academic and social opportunities. This includes accommodations for students with disabilities, assistive technology, and disability-related counseling.

#### International Student Support

MIT has a diverse international student population, and the Institute provides support services to help these students adjust to life in the United States. This includes:

- The International Students Office (ISO): The ISO provides support services for international students, including immigration advice, cultural adjustment support, and social events.

- The English Language Center (ELC): The ELC provides English language instruction and support for international students. This includes English language courses, conversation groups, and academic writing support.

#### Student Organizations

MIT has a vibrant student organization community, with over 400 recognized student organizations. These organizations provide opportunities for students to explore their interests, develop leadership skills, and build community. Some of these organizations are specifically focused on environmental science, such as the MIT Environmental Club and the MIT Solar Electric Vehicle Team.

#### Financial Support

MIT recognizes the financial challenges that many students face, and the Institute provides financial support to help students meet these challenges. This includes:

- Financial Aid: MIT offers need-based financial aid to all undergraduate students. This includes grants, loans, and work-study opportunities.

- Scholarships: MIT offers a variety of scholarships to undergraduate students. These scholarships are based on academic merit, financial need, and other criteria.

- Work-Study: The MIT Work-Study Program provides part-time employment opportunities for undergraduate students. These jobs are on-campus and off-campus, and they offer a valuable opportunity for students to earn money while gaining valuable work experience.

#### Housing and Dining

MIT provides housing and dining services for undergraduate students. These services are designed to provide a comfortable and healthy living environment for students. Housing options include residence halls, fraternities, and off-campus apartments. Dining options include on-campus dining halls, cafes, and convenience stores.

#### Health and Safety

MIT is committed to the health and safety of its students. The Institute provides a variety of health and safety services, including:

- The MIT Police Department: The MIT Police Department provides 24-hour patrol and security services to the MIT community. This includes emergency response, crime prevention, and safety education.

- The MIT Environmental Health and Safety Office: The MIT Environmental Health and Safety Office ensures that MIT's facilities and activities are conducted in a safe and environmentally responsible manner. This includes safety training, hazardous waste management, and emergency response.

#### Other Resources

In addition to the resources mentioned above, MIT also provides a variety of other resources to support students. These include:

- The MIT Libraries: The MIT Libraries provide access to a vast collection of books, journals, and other resources. These resources are available in print and online, and they support teaching and research at MIT.

- The MIT Museum: The MIT Museum showcases the Institute's history, culture, and scientific achievements. This includes exhibits on MIT's research, technology, and art.

- The MIT Alumni Association: The MIT Alumni Association connects MIT alumni with each other and with the Institute. This includes alumni events, networking opportunities, and alumni services.
